# Text Elements
   the following experimental data are obtained for an NACA 4122
airfoil section at an angle of attack of 4°, 
calculate the center of the pressure. ^7OxuPVqP

solution:  ^kb6KdsnZ

Example 1.3 ^mGWqzmKu

Example 1.4 ^PYgHqpi4

   Consider the DC-3 shown in the fig, Just outboard of the engine nacelle, the airfoil 
chord length is 15.4 feet, At cruising velocity 188mi/h at the sea level. The moment per unit
span at the airfoil location are                   , and                     , calculate the 
                            lift per unit span and the location of the center of the pressure
                            on the airfoil ^95Vmz0k4

solution: ^fp5NLgpO

note that for a thin, symmetrical airfoil, 
the center of the pressure is the quarter 
chord location
but for the plane like NACA 4412, the airfoil 
is not symmetric, the center of the pressure
is located behind the quart-chord position ^kSVae3Tg

          in all cases, 
the force and the moment system 
is uniquely specified by giving the 
moment acting about 2 points ^3t5i93iG

2dfd15c3e2c60162c9f4218068c49474d49b1b6e: $$M_{LE}' = -3213.9 ft\space lb/ft$$
b6c8d61e7d8661c7c912ff69455015bb99a5d1e9: [[Pasted Image 20230120230125_434.png]]
